Abella < Specification "pclf".
Reading specification "pclf".


Abella < Close ty, tm.


Abella < Define ctx : olist -> prop by 
ctx nil;
nabla x, ctx (of x T :: G) := ctx G.


Abella < Define fresh : A -> B -> prop by 
nabla x, fresh x X.


Abella < Define name : A -> prop by 
nabla x, name x.


Abella < Theorem member_prune : 
forall G E, nabla x, member (E x) G -> (exists F, E = x\F).



============================
 forall G E, nabla x, member (E x) G -> (exists F, E = x\F)

member_prune < induction on 1.


IH : forall G E, nabla x, member (E x) G * -> (exists F, E = x\F)
============================
 forall G E, nabla x, member (E x) G @ -> (exists F, E = x\F)

member_prune < intros.


Variables: G E
IH : forall G E, nabla x, member (E x) G * -> (exists F, E = x\F)
H1 : member (E n1) G @
============================
 exists F, E = x\F

member_prune < case H1.

Subgoal 1:

Variables: G2 G1
IH : forall G E, nabla x, member (E x) G * -> (exists F, E = x\F)
============================
 exists F, z1\G1 = x\F

Subgoal 2 is:
 exists F, E = x\F

member_prune < search.

Subgoal 2:

Variables: E G2 G1
IH : forall G E, nabla x, member (E x) G * -> (exists F, E = x\F)
H2 : member (E n1) G2 *
============================
 exists F, E = x\F

member_prune < apply IH to H2.

Subgoal 2:

Variables: G2 G1 F
IH : forall G E, nabla x, member (E x) G * -> (exists F, E = x\F)
H2 : member F G2 *
============================
 exists F1, z1\F = x\F1

member_prune < search.
Proof completed.

Abella < Theorem ctx_mem : 
forall G E, ctx G -> member E G -> (exists X T, E = of X T /\ fresh X T).



============================
 forall G E, ctx G -> member E G -> (exists X T, E = of X T /\ fresh X T)

ctx_mem < induction on 1.


IH : forall G E, ctx G * -> member E G ->
       (exists X T, E = of X T /\ fresh X T)
============================
 forall G E, ctx G @ -> member E G -> (exists X T, E = of X T /\ fresh X T)

ctx_mem < intros.


Variables: G E
IH : forall G E, ctx G * -> member E G ->
       (exists X T, E = of X T /\ fresh X T)
H1 : ctx G @
H2 : member E G
============================
 exists X T, E = of X T /\ fresh X T

ctx_mem < case H1.

Subgoal 1:

Variables: E
IH : forall G E, ctx G * -> member E G ->
       (exists X T, E = of X T /\ fresh X T)
H2 : member E nil
============================
 exists X T, E = of X T /\ fresh X T

Subgoal 2 is:
 exists X T, E n1 = of X T /\ fresh X T

ctx_mem < case H2.

Subgoal 2:

Variables: E G1 T
IH : forall G E, ctx G * -> member E G ->
       (exists X T, E = of X T /\ fresh X T)
H2 : member (E n1) (of n1 T :: G1)
H3 : ctx G1 *
============================
 exists X T, E n1 = of X T /\ fresh X T

ctx_mem < case H2.

Subgoal 2.1:

Variables: G1 T
IH : forall G E, ctx G * -> member E G ->
       (exists X T, E = of X T /\ fresh X T)
H3 : ctx G1 *
============================
 exists X T1, of n1 T = of X T1 /\ fresh X T1

Subgoal 2.2 is:
 exists X T, E n1 = of X T /\ fresh X T

ctx_mem < search.

Subgoal 2.2:

Variables: E G1 T
IH : forall G E, ctx G * -> member E G ->
       (exists X T, E = of X T /\ fresh X T)
H3 : ctx G1 *
H4 : member (E n1) G1
============================
 exists X T, E n1 = of X T /\ fresh X T

ctx_mem < apply IH to *H3 *H4.

Subgoal 2.2:

Variables: G1 T X T1
IH : forall G E, ctx G * -> member E G ->
       (exists X T, E = of X T /\ fresh X T)
H5 : fresh (X n1) T1
============================
 exists X1 T, of (X n1) T1 = of X1 T /\ fresh X1 T

ctx_mem < search.
Proof completed.

Abella < Theorem ctx_uniq : 
forall G X T1 T2, ctx G -> member (of X T1) G -> member (of X T2) G -> T1 =
T2.



============================
 forall G X T1 T2, ctx G -> member (of X T1) G -> member (of X T2) G -> T1 =
 T2

ctx_uniq < induction on 2.


IH : forall G X T1 T2, ctx G -> member (of X T1) G * -> member (of X T2) G ->
       T1 =
     T2
============================
 forall G X T1 T2, ctx G -> member (of X T1) G @ -> member (of X T2) G ->
   T1 =
 T2

ctx_uniq < intros.


Variables: G X T1 T2
IH : forall G X T1 T2, ctx G -> member (of X T1) G * -> member (of X T2) G ->
       T1 =
     T2
H1 : ctx G
H2 : member (of X T1) G @
H3 : member (of X T2) G
============================
 T1 = T2

ctx_uniq < case H2.

Subgoal 1:

Variables: X T1 T2 L
IH : forall G X T1 T2, ctx G -> member (of X T1) G * -> member (of X T2) G ->
       T1 =
     T2
H1 : ctx (of X T1 :: L)
H3 : member (of X T2) (of X T1 :: L)
============================
 T1 = T2

Subgoal 2 is:
 T1 = T2

ctx_uniq < case H3.

Subgoal 1.1:

Variables: X T1 L
IH : forall G X T1 T2, ctx G -> member (of X T1) G * -> member (of X T2) G ->
       T1 =
     T2
H1 : ctx (of X T1 :: L)
============================
 T1 = T1

Subgoal 1.2 is:
 T1 = T2

Subgoal 2 is:
 T1 = T2

ctx_uniq < search.

Subgoal 1.2:

Variables: X T1 T2 L
IH : forall G X T1 T2, ctx G -> member (of X T1) G * -> member (of X T2) G ->
       T1 =
     T2
H1 : ctx (of X T1 :: L)
H4 : member (of X T2) L
============================
 T1 = T2

Subgoal 2 is:
 T1 = T2

ctx_uniq < case H1.

Subgoal 1.2:

Variables: T1 T2 G1
IH : forall G X T1 T2, ctx G -> member (of X T1) G * -> member (of X T2) G ->
       T1 =
     T2
H4 : member (of n1 T2) G1
H5 : ctx G1
============================
 T1 = T2

Subgoal 2 is:
 T1 = T2

ctx_uniq < apply member_prune to H4.

Subgoal 2:

Variables: X T1 T2 L B
IH : forall G X T1 T2, ctx G -> member (of X T1) G * -> member (of X T2) G ->
       T1 =
     T2
H1 : ctx (B :: L)
H3 : member (of X T2) (B :: L)
H4 : member (of X T1) L *
============================
 T1 = T2

ctx_uniq < case H3.

Subgoal 2.1:

Variables: X T1 T2 L
IH : forall G X T1 T2, ctx G -> member (of X T1) G * -> member (of X T2) G ->
       T1 =
     T2
H1 : ctx (of X T2 :: L)
H4 : member (of X T1) L *
============================
 T1 = T2

Subgoal 2.2 is:
 T1 = T2

ctx_uniq < case H1.

Subgoal 2.1:

Variables: T1 T2 G1
IH : forall G X T1 T2, ctx G -> member (of X T1) G * -> member (of X T2) G ->
       T1 =
     T2
H4 : member (of n1 T1) G1 *
H5 : ctx G1
============================
 T1 = T2

Subgoal 2.2 is:
 T1 = T2

ctx_uniq < apply member_prune to H4.

Subgoal 2.2:

Variables: X T1 T2 L B
IH : forall G X T1 T2, ctx G -> member (of X T1) G * -> member (of X T2) G ->
       T1 =
     T2
H1 : ctx (B :: L)
H4 : member (of X T1) L *
H5 : member (of X T2) L
============================
 T1 = T2

ctx_uniq < case H1.

Subgoal 2.2:

Variables: X T1 T2 G1 T
IH : forall G X T1 T2, ctx G -> member (of X T1) G * -> member (of X T2) G ->
       T1 =
     T2
H4 : member (of (X n1) T1) G1 *
H5 : member (of (X n1) T2) G1
H6 : ctx G1
============================
 T1 = T2

ctx_uniq < apply IH to H6 H4 H5.

Subgoal 2.2:

Variables: X T2 G1 T
IH : forall G X T1 T2, ctx G -> member (of X T1) G * -> member (of X T2) G ->
       T1 =
     T2
H4 : member (of (X n1) T2) G1 *
H5 : member (of (X n1) T2) G1
H6 : ctx G1
============================
 T2 = T2

ctx_uniq < search.
Proof completed.

Abella < Theorem ty_closed : 
forall G T, ctx G -> {G |- ty T} -> {ty T}.



============================
 forall G T, ctx G -> {G |- ty T} -> {ty T}

ty_closed < induction on 2.


IH : forall G T, ctx G -> {G |- ty T}* -> {ty T}
============================
 forall G T, ctx G -> {G |- ty T}@ -> {ty T}

ty_closed < intros.


Variables: G T
IH : forall G T, ctx G -> {G |- ty T}* -> {ty T}
H1 : ctx G
H2 : {G |- ty T}@
============================

Subgoal 4 is:

 {ty (arr S T1)}

 {ty T}

Abella < Define ofsub : olist -> olist -> olist -> prop by 
ofsub G nil nil := ctx G;
nabla x, ofsub (G x) (cp x (M x) :: SS x) (of x T :: D) := nabla x, {G x |- of (M x) T} /\ ofsub (G x) (SS x) D.


Abella < Theorem ofsub_ctx : 
forall G SS D, ofsub G SS D -> ctx G /\ ctx D.



============================
 forall G SS D, ofsub G SS D -> ctx G /\ ctx D

ofsub_ctx < induction on 1.


IH : forall G SS D, ofsub G SS D * -> ctx G /\ ctx D
============================
 forall G SS D, ofsub G SS D @ -> ctx G /\ ctx D

ofsub_ctx < intros.


Variables: G SS D
IH : forall G SS D, ofsub G SS D * -> ctx G /\ ctx D
H1 : ofsub G SS D @
============================
 ctx G /\ ctx D

ofsub_ctx < case H1.

Subgoal 1:

Variables: G
IH : forall G SS D, ofsub G SS D * -> ctx G /\ ctx D
H2 : ctx G
============================
 ctx G /\ ctx nil

Subgoal 2 is:
 ctx (G n1) /\ ctx (of n1 T :: D1)

ofsub_ctx < search.

Subgoal 2:

Variables: G D1 T SS1 M
IH : forall G SS D, ofsub G SS D * -> ctx G /\ ctx D
H2 : {G n1 |- of (M n1) T}
H3 : ofsub (G n1) (SS1 n1) D1 *
============================
 ctx (G n1) /\ ctx (of n1 T :: D1)

ofsub_ctx < apply IH to H3.

Subgoal 2:

Variables: G D1 T SS1 M
IH : forall G SS D, ofsub G SS D * -> ctx G /\ ctx D
H2 : {G n1 |- of (M n1) T}
H3 : ofsub (G n1) (SS1 n1) D1 *
H4 : ctx (G n1)
H5 : ctx D1
============================
 ctx (G n1) /\ ctx (of n1 T :: D1)

ofsub_ctx < search.
Proof completed.

Abella < Theorem ofsub_weak1 :

============================

ofsub_weak1 < induction on 1.


IH : forall G SS D T, nabla x, ofsub G SS D * -> ofsub (of x T :: G) SS D
============================

ofsub_weak1 < intros.


Variables: G SS D T
IH : forall G SS D T, nabla x, ofsub G SS D * -> ofsub (of x T :: G) SS D
H1 : ofsub G SS D @
============================
 ofsub (of n1 T :: G) SS D

ofsub_weak1 < case H1.

Subgoal 1:

Variables: G T
IH : forall G SS D T, nabla x, ofsub G SS D * -> ofsub (of x T :: G) SS D
H2 : ctx G
============================
 ofsub (of n1 T :: G) nil nil

Subgoal 2 is:
 ofsub (of n1 T :: G n2) (cp n2 (M n2) :: SS1 n2) (of n2 T1 :: D1)

ofsub_weak1 < search.

Subgoal 2:

Variables: G T D1 T1 SS1 M
IH : forall G SS D T, nabla x, ofsub G SS D * -> ofsub (of x T :: G) SS D
H2 : {G n1 |- of (M n1) T1}
H3 : ofsub (G n1) (SS1 n1) D1 *
============================

ofsub_weak1 < apply IH to *H3 with T = T.

Subgoal 2:

H2 : {G n1 |- of (M n1) T1}
H4 : ofsub (of n2 T :: G n1) (SS1 n1) D1
============================

ofsub_weak1 < search.
Proof completed.

Abella < Theorem ofsub_mem_sub : 
forall G SS D E, ofsub G SS D -> member E SS ->
  (exists X M T, E = cp X M /\ member (of X T) D /\ name X /\ {G |- of M T}).



============================
 forall G SS D E, ofsub G SS D -> member E SS ->
   (exists X M T, E = cp X M /\ member (of X T) D /\ name X /\ {G |- of M T})

ofsub_mem_sub < induction on 1.


IH : forall G SS D E, ofsub G SS D * -> member E SS ->
       (exists X M T, E = cp X M /\ member (of X T) D /\ name X /\
            {G |- of M T})
============================
 forall G SS D E, ofsub G SS D @ -> member E SS ->
   (exists X M T, E = cp X M /\ member (of X T) D /\ name X /\ {G |- of M T})

ofsub_mem_sub < intros.


Variables: G SS D E
IH : forall G SS D E, ofsub G SS D * -> member E SS ->
       (exists X M T, E = cp X M /\ member (of X T) D /\ name X /\
            {G |- of M T})
H1 : ofsub G SS D @
H2 : member E SS
============================
 exists X M T, E = cp X M /\ member (of X T) D /\ name X /\ {G |- of M T}

ofsub_mem_sub < case H1.

Subgoal 1:

Variables: G E
IH : forall G SS D E, ofsub G SS D * -> member E SS ->
       (exists X M T, E = cp X M /\ member (of X T) D /\ name X /\
            {G |- of M T})
H2 : member E nil
H3 : ctx G
============================
 exists X M T, E = cp X M /\ member (of X T) nil /\ name X /\ {G |- of M T}

Subgoal 2 is:
 exists X M T1, E n1 = cp X M /\ member (of X T1) (of n1 T :: D1) /\
   name X /\ {G n1 |- of M T1}

ofsub_mem_sub < case H2.

Subgoal 2:

Variables: G E D1 T SS1 M
IH : forall G SS D E, ofsub G SS D * -> member E SS ->
       (exists X M T, E = cp X M /\ member (of X T) D /\ name X /\
            {G |- of M T})
H2 : member (E n1) (cp n1 (M n1) :: SS1 n1)
H3 : {G n1 |- of (M n1) T}
H4 : ofsub (G n1) (SS1 n1) D1 *
============================
 exists X M T1, E n1 = cp X M /\ member (of X T1) (of n1 T :: D1) /\
   name X /\ {G n1 |- of M T1}

ofsub_mem_sub < case H2.

Subgoal 2.1:

Variables: G D1 T SS1 M
IH : forall G SS D E, ofsub G SS D * -> member E SS ->
       (exists X M T, E = cp X M /\ member (of X T) D /\ name X /\
            {G |- of M T})
H3 : {G n1 |- of (M n1) T}
H4 : ofsub (G n1) (SS1 n1) D1 *
============================
 exists X M1 T1, cp n1 (M n1) = cp X M1 /\
   member (of X T1) (of n1 T :: D1) /\ name X /\ {G n1 |- of M1 T1}

Subgoal 2.2 is:
 exists X M T1, E n1 = cp X M /\ member (of X T1) (of n1 T :: D1) /\
   name X /\ {G n1 |- of M T1}

ofsub_mem_sub < search.

Subgoal 2.2:

Variables: G E D1 T SS1 M
IH : forall G SS D E, ofsub G SS D * -> member E SS ->
       (exists X M T, E = cp X M /\ member (of X T) D /\ name X /\
            {G |- of M T})
H3 : {G n1 |- of (M n1) T}
H4 : ofsub (G n1) (SS1 n1) D1 *
H5 : member (E n1) (SS1 n1)
============================
 exists X M T1, E n1 = cp X M /\ member (of X T1) (of n1 T :: D1) /\
   name X /\ {G n1 |- of M T1}

ofsub_mem_sub < apply IH to *H4 *H5.

Subgoal 2.2:

Variables: G D1 T SS1 M X M1 T1
IH : forall G SS D E, ofsub G SS D * -> member E SS ->
       (exists X M T, E = cp X M /\ member (of X T) D /\ name X /\
            {G |- of M T})
H3 : {G n1 |- of (M n1) T}
H6 : member (of (X n1) T1) D1
H7 : name (X n1)
H8 : {G n1 |- of (M1 n1) T1}
============================
 exists X1 M T1, cp (X n1) (M1 n1) = cp X1 M /\
   member (of X1 T1) (of n1 T :: D1) /\ name X1 /\ {G n1 |- of M T1}

ofsub_mem_sub < search.
Proof completed.

Abella < Theorem ofsub_mem_src :

Variables: G E D1 T SS1 M
IH : forall G SS D E, ofsub G SS D * -> member E D ->
       (exists X M T, E = of X T /\ member (cp X M) SS /\ name X /\
            {G |- of M T})
H3 : {G n1 |- of (M n1) T}
H4 : ofsub (G n1) (SS1 n1) D1 *
H5 : member (E n1) D1
============================
 exists X M1 T, E n1 = of X T /\ member (cp X M1) (cp n1 (M n1) :: SS1 n1) /\
   name X /\ {G n1 |- of M1 T}

ofsub_mem_src < apply IH to *H4 *H5.

Subgoal 2.2:

Variables: G D1 T SS1 M X M1 T1
IH : forall G SS D E, ofsub G SS D * -> member E D ->
       (exists X M T, E = of X T /\ member (cp X M) SS /\ name X /\
            {G |- of M T})
H3 : {G n1 |- of (M n1) T}
H6 : member (cp (X n1) (M1 n1)) (SS1 n1)
H7 : name (X n1)
H8 : {G n1 |- of (M1 n1) T1}
============================
 exists X1 M1 T, of (X n1) T1 = of X1 T /\
   member (cp X1 M1) (cp n1 (M n1) :: SS1 n1) /\ name X1 /\ {G n1 |- of M1 T}

ofsub_mem_src < search.
Proof completed.

Abella < Theorem ofsub_sub_prune : 
forall G SS D, nabla x, ofsub (G x) SS (D x) -> (exists DD, D = x\DD).



============================
 forall G SS D, nabla x, ofsub (G x) SS (D x) -> (exists DD, D = x\DD)

ofsub_sub_prune < induction on 1.


IH : forall G SS D, nabla x, ofsub (G x) SS (D x) * -> (exists DD, D = x\DD)
============================
 forall G SS D, nabla x, ofsub (G x) SS (D x) @ -> (exists DD, D = x\DD)

ofsub_sub_prune < intros.


Variables: G SS D
IH : forall G SS D, nabla x, ofsub (G x) SS (D x) * -> (exists DD, D = x\DD)
H1 : ofsub (G n1) SS (D n1) @
============================
 exists DD, D = x\DD

ofsub_sub_prune < case H1.

Subgoal 1:

Variables: G
IH : forall G SS D, nabla x, ofsub (G x) SS (D x) * -> (exists DD, D = x\DD)
H2 : ctx (G n1)
============================
 exists DD, z1\nil = x\DD

Subgoal 2 is:
 exists DD, z2\of n2 T :: D1 z2 = x\DD

ofsub_sub_prune < search.

Subgoal 2:

Variables: G D1 T SS3 SS2
IH : forall G SS D, nabla x, ofsub (G x) SS (D x) * -> (exists DD, D = x\DD)
H2 : {G n2 n1 |- of (SS2 n2) T}
H3 : ofsub (G n2 n1) (SS3 n2) (D1 n1) *
============================
 exists DD, z2\of n2 T :: D1 z2 = x\DD

ofsub_sub_prune < apply IH to H3.

Subgoal 2:

Variables: G T SS3 SS2 DD
IH : forall G SS D, nabla x, ofsub (G x) SS (D x) * -> (exists DD, D = x\DD)
H2 : {G n2 n1 |- of (SS2 n2) T}
H3 : ofsub (G n2 n1) (SS3 n2) DD *
============================
 exists DD1, z2\of n2 T :: DD = x\DD1

ofsub_sub_prune < search.
Proof completed.

Abella < Theorem subst : 
forall G SS D M T, ofsub G SS D -> {D |- of M T} ->
  (exists SM, {SS |- cp M SM} /\ {G |- of SM T}).



============================
 forall G SS D M T, ofsub G SS D -> {D |- of M T} ->
   (exists SM, {SS |- cp M SM} /\ {G |- of SM T})

subst < induction on 2.


IH : forall G SS D M T, ofsub G SS D -> {D |- of M T}* ->
       (exists SM, {SS |- cp M SM} /\ {G |- of SM T})
============================
 forall G SS D M T, ofsub G SS D -> {D |- of M T}@ ->
   (exists SM, {SS |- cp M SM} /\ {G |- of SM T})

subst < intros.

       (exists SM, {SS |- cp M SM} /\ {G |- of SM T})

subst < case H2.

Abella < Theorem ofsub_det : 
forall G SS D X M1 M2, ofsub G SS D -> member (cp X M1) SS ->
  member (cp X M2) SS -> M1 =
M2.



============================
 forall G SS D X M1 M2, ofsub G SS D -> member (cp X M1) SS ->
   member (cp X M2) SS -> M1 =
 M2

ofsub_det < induction on 1.


IH : forall G SS D X M1 M2, ofsub G SS D * -> member (cp X M1) SS ->
       member (cp X M2) SS -> M1 =
     M2
============================

   member (cp X M2) SS -> M1 =
 M2

       member (cp X M2) SS -> M1 =
     M2

H2 : member (cp X M1) SS
H3 : member (cp X M2) SS
============================
 M1 = M2

ofsub_det < case H1.

Abella < Theorem cp_det : 
forall G SS D M N1 N2, ofsub G SS D -> {SS |- cp M N1} -> {SS |- cp M N2} ->
  N1 =
N2.



============================
 forall G SS D M N1 N2, ofsub G SS D -> {SS |- cp M N1} -> {SS |- cp M N2} ->
   N1 =
 N2

cp_det < induction on 2.


IH : forall G SS D M N1 N2, ofsub G SS D -> {SS |- cp M N1}* ->
       {SS |- cp M N2} -> N1 =
     N2
============================
 forall G SS D M N1 N2, ofsub G SS D -> {SS |- cp M N1}@ ->
   {SS |- cp M N2} -> N1 =
 N2

cp_det < intros.


Variables: G SS D M N1 N2
IH : forall G SS D M N1 N2, ofsub G SS D -> {SS |- cp M N1}* ->
       {SS |- cp M N2} -> N1 =
     N2
H1 : ofsub G SS D
H2 : {SS |- cp M N1}@
H3 : {SS |- cp M N2}
============================
 N1 = N2

cp_det < case H2.

Subgoal 1:

Variables: G SS D N2
IH : forall G SS D M N1 N2, ofsub G SS D -> {SS |- cp M N1}* ->
       {SS |- cp M N2} -> N1 =
     N2
H1 : ofsub G SS D
H3 : {SS |- cp zero N2}
============================

Abella < Define comp : olist -> olist -> olist -> prop by 
comp SS nil nil;
nabla x, comp (SS x) (cp x (M x) :: TT x) (cp x (N x) :: UU x) := nabla x, {SS x |- cp (M x) (N x)} /\ comp (SS x) (TT x) (UU x).


Abella < Theorem comp_weak :

Abella < Theorem compose_var_lemma : 
forall G SS D TT W UU M N, nabla x, ofsub (G x) (SS x) (D x) ->

  member (cp x (M x)) (TT x) -> {SS x |- cp (M x) (N x)} ->
  {UU x |- cp x (N x)}.



============================

   ofsub (D x) (TT x) (W x) -> comp (SS x) (TT x) (UU x) ->
   member (cp x (M x)) (TT x) -> {SS x |- cp (M x) (N x)} ->
   {UU x |- cp x (N x)}

Proof completed.

Abella < Theorem compose_map : 
forall G SS D TT W UU M N K T, ofsub G SS D -> ofsub D TT W ->
  comp SS TT UU -> {W |- of M T} -> {TT |- cp M N} -> {SS |- cp N K} ->
  {UU |- cp M K}.



============================
 forall G SS D TT W UU M N K T, ofsub G SS D -> ofsub D TT W ->
   comp SS TT UU -> {W |- of M T} -> {TT |- cp M N} -> {SS |- cp N K} ->
   {UU |- cp M K}

compose_map < induction on 4.


IH : forall G SS D TT W UU M N K T, ofsub G SS D -> ofsub D TT W ->
       comp SS TT UU -> {W |- of M T}* -> {TT |- cp M N} -> {SS |- cp N K} ->
       {UU |- cp M K}

   comp SS TT UU -> {W |- of M T}@ -> {TT |- cp M N} -> {SS |- cp N K} ->
   {UU |- cp M K}

compose_map < intros.

Abella < Theorem compose_exists : 
forall G SS D TT W, ofsub G SS D -> ofsub D TT W ->
  (exists UU, comp SS TT UU /\ ofsub G UU W).



============================
 forall G SS D TT W, ofsub G SS D -> ofsub D TT W ->
   (exists UU, comp SS TT UU /\ ofsub G UU W)

compose_exists < induction on 2.


IH : forall G SS D TT W, ofsub G SS D -> ofsub D TT W * ->
       (exists UU, comp SS TT UU /\ ofsub G UU W)
============================
 forall G SS D TT W, ofsub G SS D -> ofsub D TT W @ ->
   (exists UU, comp SS TT UU /\ ofsub G UU W)

compose_exists < intros.

       (exists UU, comp SS TT UU /\ ofsub G UU W)

============================

Abella < Theorem compose : 
forall G SS D TT W M N K T, ofsub G SS D -> ofsub D TT W -> {W |- of M T} ->

   (exists UU, ofsub G UU W /\ {UU |- cp M K})

Proof completed.

Abella < Theorem ofsub_strength : 
forall G SS D DD, ctx D -> ctx DD -> (forall E, member E D -> member E DD) ->
  ofsub G SS DD ->
  (exists TT, ofsub G TT D /\
       (forall E, member E SS -> member E TT \/
            (exists X M, E = cp X M /\ fresh X D))).



============================
 forall G SS D DD, ctx D -> ctx DD ->
   (forall E, member E D -> member E DD) -> ofsub G SS DD ->
   (exists TT, ofsub G TT D /\
        (forall E, member E SS -> member E TT \/
             (exists X M, E = cp X M /\ fresh X D)))

IH : forall G SS D DD, ctx D * -> ctx DD ->
       (forall E, member E D -> member E DD) -> ofsub G SS DD ->

            (forall E, member E SS -> member E TT \/
                 (exists X M, E = cp X M /\ fresh X D)))

   (exists TT, ofsub G TT D /\
        (forall E, member E SS -> member E TT \/
             (exists X M, E = cp X M /\ fresh X D)))

ofsub_strength < intros.

forall G SS D M N T TT, ofsub G SS D -> {D |- of M T} ->
  (forall E, member E TT -> member E SS \/

  {TT |- cp M N} -> {SS |- cp M N}.



============================

   (forall E, member E TT -> member E SS \/
        (exists X M, E = cp X M /\ fresh X D)) ->
   {TT |- cp M N} -> {SS |- cp M N}
